# ttnn.to_device

| Name | Input Shapes | Input Layouts | Attributes | Output Shapes | Output Layouts |
|------|--------------|---------------|------------|---------------|----------------|
| ttnn.to_device | tensor<[32000,4096,bf16]> <br> !tt.device<#device> | mapping_from: ('d0', 'd1'), mapping_to: ('d0', 'd1'), memory_config: (32000, 4096, 'bf16', 'system') | memory_config: #ttnn.memory_config<<interleaved>, <dram>, <<1000x128>>> | tensor<[32000,4096,bf16]> | mapping_from: ('d0', 'd1'), mapping_to: ('d0', 'd1'), memory_config: (1000, 128, 'tile<32x32, bf16>', 'dram') |
